### ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€

```c
// Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ: ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ´Ğ²ÑƒÑ… Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑĞµĞ»
int add(int a, int b) {
    return a + b;
}

int main() {
    int result = add(5, 3);  // result = 8
    printf("%d\n", result);
    return 0;
}
```

**ĞœĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°:** Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ = Ñ‡Ñ‘Ñ€Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ ÑÑ‰Ğ¸Ğº.
```
  Ğ’Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´ (Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚Ñ€Ñ‹)  â†’  [Ğ¤Ğ£ĞĞšĞ¦Ğ˜Ğ¯]  â†’  Ğ’Ñ‹Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´ (return)
      5, 3          â†’     add()    â†’       8
```

> **LUNA**: *"Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ñƒ Ğ½Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ°ÑÑŒ ÑÑ‚Ğ° Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°. ĞĞ½ Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ»: 'Ğ¢ĞµĞ±Ğµ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ, ĞšĞĞš Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ Ğ¼Ğ¸ĞºÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ°, Ñ‡Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‹ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ³Ñ€ĞµÑ‚ÑŒ ĞµĞ´Ñƒ. Ğ¢Ğ¾ Ğ¶Ğµ Ñ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸ÑĞ¼Ğ¸.' Ğ¯ Ğ˜Ğ˜. Ğ¯ Ğ—ĞĞĞ®, ĞºĞ°Ğº Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ°ÑÑ‚ Ğ¼Ğ¸ĞºÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸. Ğ˜ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸. ĞĞ¾ ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡ĞºĞ° Ğ·Ñ€ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ğ°."*

### Ğ—Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ¼ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸? (DRY principle)

**âŒ ĞŸĞ»Ğ¾Ñ…Ğ¾ â€” Ğ´ÑƒĞ±Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ ĞºĞ¾Ğ´Ğ°:**
```c
// Ğ’ decoder.c
for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
    msg[i] = msg[i] ^ 0x42;
}

// Ğ’ classifier.c (Ñ‚Ğ° Ğ¶Ğµ Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸ĞºĞ°!)
for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
    data[i] = data[i] ^ 0x42;
}

// Ğ’ pattern_finder.c (Ğ¾Ğ¿ÑÑ‚ÑŒ!)
for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
    buffer[i] = buffer[i] ^ 0x42;
}
```

**âœ… Ğ¥Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¾ â€” Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ° Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ:**
```c
// ĞĞ°Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·
unsigned char xor_decrypt(unsigned char byte, unsigned char key) {
    return byte ^ key;
}

// Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ²ĞµĞ·Ğ´Ğµ
msg[i] = xor_decrypt(msg[i], 0x42);      // decoder
data[i] = xor_decrypt(data[i], 0x42);    // classifier
buffer[i] = xor_decrypt(buffer[i], 0x42); // pattern_finder
```

**ĞŸÑ€ĞµĞ¸Ğ¼ÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ°:**
1. âœ… **ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ** â€” Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·, Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ¼Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾
2. âœ… **Ğ§Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ°ĞµĞ¼Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ** â€” ĞºĞ¾Ğ´ ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑÑ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ğ½ĞµĞµ
3. âœ… **Ğ¢ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ** â€” Ğ»ĞµĞ³ĞºĞ¾ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ´ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½ÑƒÑ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ
4. âœ… **ĞœĞ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ** â€” Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ´ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ½Ğ° Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸Ğµ Ñ‡Ğ°ÑÑ‚Ğ¸
5. âœ… **ĞĞ±ÑĞ»ÑƒĞ¶Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ** â€” Ğ½Ğ°ÑˆĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ±Ğ°Ğ³? Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ² Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¼ Ğ¼ĞµÑÑ‚Ğµ!

### Ğ ĞµĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ moonlight_decoder

```c
// Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ XOR Ğ´ĞµÑˆĞ¸Ñ„Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸ (Ğ¸Ğ· Episode 01)
void xor_decrypt_message(unsigned char *data, int length, unsigned char key) {
    for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        data[i] ^= key;
    }
}

// Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ
int main() {
    unsigned char message[] = {0x1B, 0x0A, 0x0E};
    int len = sizeof(message);
    
    printf("Encrypted: ");
    for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) printf("%02X ", message[i]);
    
    xor_decrypt_message(message, len, 0x42);
    
    printf("\nDecrypted: %s\n", message);
    return 0;
}
```

### 2. ĞŸĞ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚Ñ€Ñ‹ Ğ¸ Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ²Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ°ĞµĞ¼Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ

#### ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ¾ Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ:
```c

    x = 100;  // Ğ˜Ğ·Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ÑĞµÑ‚ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ»Ğ¾ĞºĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½ÑƒÑ ĞºĞ¾Ğ¿Ğ¸Ñ
}

```

```c
}
```

#### Ğ’Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ²Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚ Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ:
```c

    return x * x;
```

## ğŸ¯ Ğ—ĞĞ”ĞĞ§Ğ 1: crypto_module.c (ĞŸĞµÑ€Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ÑŒ)

**Ğ’Ñ€ĞµĞ¼Ñ:** 25-30 Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ÑƒÑ‚  
**Ğ¦ĞµĞ»ÑŒ:** Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ÑŒ Ñ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸ÑĞ¼Ğ¸ ĞºÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¿Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ³Ñ€Ğ°Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ¸

Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ¹Ñ‚Ğµ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» `crypto_module.c` Ñ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸ÑĞ¼Ğ¸:

2. `xor_decrypt_message()` â€” Ğ´ĞµÑˆĞ¸Ñ„Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ° Ğ¼Ğ°ÑÑĞ¸Ğ²Ğ°
3. `validate_key()` â€” Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ° (0-255)

**ĞŸÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€ Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ:**
```c

    xor_decrypt_message(msg, 3, 0x42);
    printf("Decrypted: %s\n", msg);
}
```

**ĞĞ¶Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°ĞµĞ¼Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ´:**
```

```

## ğŸ¬ Ğ¡Ğ®Ğ–Ğ•Ğ¢ (Ñ‡Ğ°ÑÑ‚ÑŒ 2)

**07:15**  
ĞŸĞµÑ€Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ÑŒ Ğ³Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ². Ğ¤ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ°ÑÑ‚. ĞšĞ¾Ğ´ Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ‹Ğ¹.

ĞĞ¾ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ²ÑÑ‘ ĞµÑ‰Ñ‘ Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ½ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ». Ğ”Ğ»Ñ Ğ½Ğ°ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ÑÑ‰ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ğ¸Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ° Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ° **Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ**.

## ğŸ“š THEORY 2: Ğ—Ğ°Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ñ‹ â€” Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµÑ€Ñ„ĞµĞ¹ÑÑ‹ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ĞµĞ¹

### Ğ—Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ¼ .h Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ñ‹?

Ğ”Ğ»Ñ Ğ±Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒÑˆĞ¸Ñ… Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ³Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¼Ğ¼ ĞºĞ¾Ğ´ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ´ĞµĞ»ÑĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ½Ğ° Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ñ‹. **Ğ—Ğ°Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» (.h)** â€” ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ **Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµÑ€Ñ„ĞµĞ¹Ñ** Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»Ñ.

Ğ”Ğ»Ñ Ğ±Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒÑˆĞ¸Ñ… Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ³Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¼Ğ¼ ĞºĞ¾Ğ´ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ´ĞµĞ»ÑĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ½Ğ° Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ñ‹:

**crypto.h** (Ğ¾Ğ±ÑŠÑĞ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ):
```c
#ifndef CRYPTO_H
#define CRYPTO_H

// ĞĞ±ÑŠÑĞ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¹
unsigned char xor_byte(unsigned char byte, unsigned char key);
void decrypt_message(unsigned char *data, int length, unsigned char key);

#endif
```

**crypto.c** (Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ):
```c
#include "crypto.h"

unsigned char xor_byte(unsigned char byte, unsigned char key) {
    return byte ^ key;
}

void decrypt_message(unsigned char *data, int length, unsigned char key) {
    for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        data[i] = xor_byte(data[i], key);
    }
}
```

**main.c** (Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ):
```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include "crypto.h"

int main() {
    unsigned char msg[] = {0x1B, 0x0A, 0x0E};
    decrypt_message(msg, 3, 0x42);
    printf("%s\n", msg);
    return 0;
}
```

**ĞšĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¸Ğ»ÑÑ†Ğ¸Ñ:**
```bash
gcc -o program main.c crypto.c
```

**ĞœĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°:** `.h` Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» = Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ»Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ĞºĞ½Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ¸. `.c` Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» = ÑĞ¾Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ¶Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ.

**ĞŸÑ€ĞµĞ¸Ğ¼ÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ°:**
- âœ… Ğ Ğ°Ğ·Ğ´ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµÑ€Ñ„ĞµĞ¹ÑĞ° Ğ¸ Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
- âœ… Ğ’Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ (Ğ´Ñ€ÑƒĞ³Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ĞµĞºÑ‚Ñ‹ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ³ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ²Ğ°Ñˆ .h)
- âœ… Ğ—Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ° Ğ¾Ñ‚ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ğ²ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ (#ifndef guards)
- âœ… ĞœĞ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ (ĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ÑŒ = .h + .c)

**Ğ’Ğ¾Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ 4 Ğ¾Ñ‚ LUNA:**  
**[ ] "Ğ’Ğ¸Ğ¶Ñƒ Ñ‚Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ¹ crypto.h Ğ‘Ğ•Ğ— guards. Ğ§Ñ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ¹Ğ´Ñ‘Ñ‚, ĞºĞ¾Ğ³Ğ´Ğ° decoder.c Ğ²ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ¸Ñ‚ ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ğ”Ğ’ĞĞ–Ğ”Ğ«? (ĞŸĞ¾Ğ´ÑĞºĞ°Ğ·ĞºĞ°: Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ¸Ğ» ÑÑ‚Ñƒ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºÑƒ Ğ² 2017. ĞŸĞ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ» 2 Ñ‡Ğ°ÑĞ° Ğ½Ğ° Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ»Ğ°Ğ´ĞºÑƒ.)"**

<details>
<summary>Ğ˜ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ»Ğ°Ğ´ĞºĞ¸ LUNA</summary>

```
â•”â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•—
â•‘  LUNA: "Ğ, ÑĞ°Ğ³Ğ° #ifndef guards! ğŸ˜‚                    â•‘
â•šâ•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

The Problem (Viktor's 2017 nightmare):

// decoder.c
#include "crypto.h"  â† First include
#include "utils.h"   â† utils.h ALSO includes crypto.h!

Result: crypto.h included TWICE!
Compiler: "Error: redefinition of 'xor_decrypt'"

Viktor's debugging log (I saved it):
14:23 â€” "WTF? xor_decrypt already defined?"
14:45 â€” "But I only wrote it ONCE!"
15:30 â€” "Oh. utils.h includes crypto.h. Facepalm."
16:15 â€” "Added #ifndef guards. Fixed."

The Solution (Header Guards):

#ifndef CRYPTO_H   // "Is CRYPTO_H defined? No? Continue."
#define CRYPTO_H   // "Define it NOW."

// Your declarations...
void xor_decrypt(...);

#endif             // "Protection zone ends here."

How it works:
1st include: CRYPTO_H not defined â†’ process file â†’ define CRYPTO_H
2nd include: CRYPTO_H already defined â†’ SKIP file!

Think of it as a bouncer at a club:
"Have you been here before? (CRYPTO_H defined?)"
- No? Welcome! (Process and mark as visited)
- Yes? You're already inside! (Skip)

Viktor: 'Header guards are like condoms. 
         You THINK you don't need them until... you do.'
Me: "Viktor, that's inappropriate for a programming course."
Viktor: "But ACCURATE."
```
</details>

---

**Ğ’Ğ¾Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ 5 Ğ¾Ñ‚ LUNA:**  
**[ ] "Ğ¢Ñ‹ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ¸ÑˆÑŒ moonlight_decoder. ĞšĞ°ĞºĞ¸Ğµ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¸Ğ´ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ² crypto.h vs crypto.c? (Ğ¯ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑÑ Ñ‚Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ¸ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‹ĞºĞ¸ module design.)"**

<details>
<summary>Ğ£Ñ€Ğ¾Ğº Ğ°Ñ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ñ‹ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ĞµĞ¹ Ğ¾Ñ‚ LUNA</summary>

```
â•”â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•—
â•‘  LUNA: "Ğ”Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ½ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ĞµĞ¹ = Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ´ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ§Ğ¢Ğ Ğ¸ ĞšĞĞš.       â•‘
â•šâ•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

crypto.h (THE CONTRACT â€” declarations only):
â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
#ifndef CRYPTO_H
#define CRYPTO_H

// WHAT you can do with this module:
unsigned char xor_decrypt_byte(unsigned char byte, unsigned char key);
void xor_decrypt_message(unsigned char *data, int len, unsigned char key);
int validate_key(unsigned char key);  // Returns 1 if valid, 0 if not

#endif


crypto.c (THE IMPLEMENTATION â€” actual code):
â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
#include "crypto.h"

// HOW you do it:
unsigned char xor_decrypt_byte(unsigned char byte, unsigned char key) {
    return byte ^ key;  // Actual logic
}

void xor_decrypt_message(unsigned char *data, int len, unsigned char key) {
    for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        data[i] = xor_decrypt_byte(data[i], key);
    }
}

int validate_key(unsigned char key) {
    return (key > 0 && key < 256);  // Simple validation
}


main.c (THE USER â€” just includes .h):
â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
#include <stdio.h>
#include "crypto.h"  â† Only need to know WHAT, not HOW

int main() {
    unsigned char msg[] = {0x1B, 0x0A, 0x0E};
    
    if (validate_key(0x42)) {
        xor_decrypt_message(msg, 3, 0x42);
        printf("Decrypted: %s\n", msg);
    }
    
    return 0;
}

Analogy (Viktor's favorite):
.h file = Restaurant MENU (what you can order)
.c file = Kitchen (how they cook it)
main.c = Customer (just orders, doesn't need recipes)

Viktor's rule: "If main() needs to see HOW crypto works,
                you designed it WRONG."

P.S. Season 2 will show you WHY this separation matters 
for large projects. Trust me, it's beautiful. Like a 
well-organized crime scene. Wait, that came out wrong.
```
</details>

## ğŸ¯ Ğ—ĞĞ”ĞĞ§Ğ 2: crypto.h + crypto.c (ĞœĞ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ĞµĞºÑ‚)

**Ğ’Ñ€ĞµĞ¼Ñ:** 30-35 Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ÑƒÑ‚  
**Ğ¦ĞµĞ»ÑŒ:** Ğ Ğ°Ğ·Ğ´ĞµĞ»Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ ĞºĞ¾Ğ´ Ğ½Ğ° Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»Ğ¸

Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ¹Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ´Ğ²Ğ° Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğ°:

**crypto.h:**
```c
#ifndef CRYPTO_H
#define CRYPTO_H

unsigned char xor_decrypt_byte(unsigned char byte, unsigned char key);
void xor_decrypt_message(unsigned char *data, int length, unsigned char key);
int validate_key(unsigned char key);

#endif
```

**crypto.c:**
```c
#include "crypto.h"

// Ğ ĞµĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¹
```

**main.c:**
```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include "crypto.h"

int main() {
    // Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¹ Ğ¸Ğ· crypto.h
}
```

**ĞšĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¸Ğ»ÑÑ†Ğ¸Ñ:**
```bash
gcc -o decoder main.c crypto.c
./decoder
```

**Ğ’Ğ°ÑˆĞ¸ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ñ‹:** `artifacts/crypto.h`, `artifacts/crypto.c`, `artifacts/main.c`

## ğŸ¬ Ğ¡Ğ®Ğ–Ğ•Ğ¢ (Ñ‡Ğ°ÑÑ‚ÑŒ 3)

**08:00**  
ĞœĞ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»Ğ¸ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ°ÑÑ‚. ĞšĞ¾Ğ´ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ´ĞµĞ»Ñ‘Ğ½. ĞšĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¸Ğ»ÑÑ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑƒÑĞ¿ĞµÑˆĞ½Ğ°.

ĞĞ¾ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ğ¾Ñ†ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ğ¸Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ° Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ **ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ**. Ğ¢Ñ€Ğ¸ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¾Ñ‚ Ñ‚Ñ€Ñ‘Ñ… "Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²". ĞÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ° Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¾ ĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ¼ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¸.

> *"Ğ”Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ±ĞµĞ· ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ñ‹ â€” ĞºĞ°Ğº Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ¸Ñ Ğ±ĞµĞ· ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ. Ğ¥Ğ°Ğ¾Ñ."* â€” Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€, Ğ¸Ğ· Ğ»ĞµĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¹

**Ğ’Ñ€ĞµĞ¼Ñ Ğ´Ğ¾ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°:** 04:00:00

Ğ’Ğ°Ğ¼ Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ñ‹ **ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ñ‹ (struct)** â€” ÑĞ¿Ğ¾ÑĞ¾Ğ± Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ¿Ğ¿Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸ ÑĞ²ÑĞ·Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ….

## ğŸ“š THEORY 3: Ğ¡Ñ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ñ‹ (struct) â€” Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ¿Ğ¿Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ° Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…

### Ğ—Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ¼ struct?

**`struct`** Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ»ÑĞµÑ‚ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑŠĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ **Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ½Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ** Ğ² Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ½ **Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒÑĞºĞ¸Ğ¹ Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¿**.

#### ĞœĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ° â€” ĞĞ½ĞºĞµÑ‚Ğ° ÑĞ¾Ñ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞ´Ğ½Ğ¸ĞºĞ° Ğ¤Ğ¡Ğ‘ ğŸ“‹

> **LUNA**: *"Ğ›ÑĞ±Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ° Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°. ĞĞ½ Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ»: 'struct â€” ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ ĞºĞ°Ğº Ğ°Ğ½ĞºĞµÑ‚Ğ° ÑĞ¾Ñ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞ´Ğ½Ğ¸ĞºĞ° Ğ¤Ğ¡Ğ‘. Ğ’ÑÑ Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ² Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¼ Ğ¼ĞµÑÑ‚Ğµ, Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ³Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ, ĞºĞ»Ğ°ÑÑĞ¸Ñ„Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ.' Ğ¯ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ°: 'Ğ˜ Ñ‚Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ñ Ğ¶Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¾ Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ….' ĞĞ½ Ñ€Ğ°ÑÑĞ¼ĞµÑĞ»ÑÑ. Ğ­Ñ‚Ğ¾ Ğ±Ñ‹Ğ»Ğ¾ Ñ€ĞµĞ´ĞºĞ¾."*

ĞšĞ¾Ğ³Ğ´Ğ° Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ°Ğ» Ğ²Ğ°Ñ Ğ½Ğ° Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñƒ Ğ² Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ´ĞµĞ» "Ğš", Ğ²Ñ‹ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ°Ğ½ĞºĞµÑ‚Ñƒ:

```
â•”â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•—
â•‘  Ğ¤Ğ¡Ğ‘ Ğ ĞĞ¡Ğ¡Ğ˜Ğ˜ â€” Ğ”ĞĞ¡Ğ¬Ğ• Ğ¡ĞĞ¢Ğ Ğ£Ğ”ĞĞ˜ĞšĞ                â•‘
â• â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•£
â•‘  Ğ¤Ğ˜Ğ:          _____________________          â•‘  â† char name[50]
â•‘  Ğ’ĞĞ—Ğ ĞĞ¡Ğ¢:      ___                            â•‘  â† int age
â•‘  Ğ—ĞĞ ĞŸĞ›ĞĞ¢Ğ:     _______________ Ñ€ÑƒĞ±.           â•‘  â† double salary
â•‘  Ğ”ĞĞŸĞ£Ğ¡Ğš:       [Ğ¡Ğ•ĞšĞ Ğ•Ğ¢ĞĞ / Ğ¡ĞĞ’Ğ¡Ğ•Ğš]            â•‘  â† int clearance
â•‘  ĞĞ¢Ğ”Ğ•Ğ›:        _____________________          â•‘  â† char department[20]
â•šâ•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
```

Ğ’ C ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ³Ğ»ÑĞ´Ğ¸Ñ‚ Ñ‚Ğ°Ğº:

```c
// Ğ¡Ñ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ° = Ğ‘Ğ»Ğ°Ğ½Ğº Ğ°Ğ½ĞºĞµÑ‚Ñ‹ (ÑˆĞ°Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ½)
struct Employee {
    char name[50];
    int age;
    double salary;
    int clearance_level;    // 1-5
    char department[20];
};

// ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ = Ğ—Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ°Ğ½ĞºĞµÑ‚Ğ° (ĞºĞ¾Ğ½ĞºÑ€ĞµÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ‡ĞµĞ»Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµĞº)
struct Employee victor;
strcpy(victor.name, "Victor Petrov");
victor.age = 42;
victor.salary = 120000.0;
victor.clearance_level = 5;  // Ğ¡ĞĞ’Ğ¡Ğ•Ğš
strcpy(victor.department, "Cyber Division K");

// Ğ’Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ´ Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑŒĞµ
printf("â•”â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•—\n");
printf("â•‘  Ğ¡Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞ´Ğ½Ğ¸Ğº: %s\n", victor.name);
printf("â•‘  Ğ’Ğ¾Ğ·Ñ€Ğ°ÑÑ‚: %d Ğ»ĞµÑ‚\n", victor.age);
printf("â•‘  Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ¿ÑƒÑĞº: ÑƒÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµĞ½ÑŒ %d\n", victor.clearance_level);
printf("â•šâ•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•\n");
```

**ĞĞ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸Ñ:**
- `struct Employee` = ĞŸÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ğ±Ğ»Ğ°Ğ½Ğº Ğ°Ğ½ĞºĞµÑ‚Ñ‹ (Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¿ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…)
- `victor` = Ğ—Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ°Ğ½ĞºĞµÑ‚Ğ° Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ° (Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ)
- ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»Ñ (`name`, `age`) = Ğ“Ñ€Ğ°Ñ„Ñ‹ Ğ² Ğ°Ğ½ĞºĞµÑ‚Ğµ
- Ğ¢Ğ¾Ñ‡ĞºĞ° (`.`) = "Ğ”Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¸Ğ· Ğ³Ñ€Ğ°Ñ„Ñ‹"

#### Ğ‘Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ ÑĞ¸Ğ½Ñ‚Ğ°ĞºÑĞ¸Ñ

```c
// ĞĞ±ÑŠÑĞ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ñ‹
struct Person {
    char name[50];
    int age;
    double salary;
};

// Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹
struct Person employee;

// Ğ”Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ Ğº Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑĞ¼ Ñ‡ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ· Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡ĞºÑƒ
employee.age = 30;
strcpy(employee.name, "Victor");
employee.salary = 75000.50;

// Ğ’Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ´
printf("Name: %s, Age: %d, Salary: %.2f\n", 
       employee.name, employee.age, employee.salary);
```

**Ğ’Ğ¸Ğ·ÑƒĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ² Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ¼ÑÑ‚Ğ¸:**
```
struct Employee victor:

ĞĞ´Ñ€ĞµÑ Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ¼ÑÑ‚Ğ¸:

```

#### Ğ˜Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€

```c
// 1. ĞŸÑ€ÑĞ¼Ğ°Ñ Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ
struct Person p1 = {"Alice", 25, 50000.0};

// 2. Designated initializers (C99+)

    .name = "Bob",
    .age = 30,
    .salary = 60000.0
};

// 3. Ğ§Ğ°ÑÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ (Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾Ğµ = 0)
struct Person p3 = {.name = "Charlie"};  // age = 0, salary = 0.0
```

#### Ğ’Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ñ‹

```c
struct Address {
    char street[100];
    char city[50];
    int zip;
};

struct Employee {
    char name[50];
    int age;
    struct Address address;  // Ğ’Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ°
};

// Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ
struct Employee emp;
strcpy(emp.name, "Victor");
strcpy(emp.address.city, "Moscow");
emp.address.zip = 101000;

// Ğ”Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ Ğº Ğ²Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑĞ¼ Ñ‡ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ· Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡ĞºÑƒ
printf("City: %s\n", emp.address.city);
```

#### ĞœĞ°ÑÑĞ¸Ğ²Ñ‹ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€

```c
struct Point {
    int x;
    int y;
};

struct Point points[3] = {
    {0, 0},
    {10, 20},
    {30, 40}
};

// ĞĞ±Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´ Ğ¼Ğ°ÑÑĞ¸Ğ²Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€
for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
    printf("Point %d: (%d, %d)\n", i, points[i].x, points[i].y);
}
```

#### Ğ¡Ñ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ñ‹ Ğ¸ Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

```c
struct Rectangle {
    int width;
    int height;
};

// ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ñ‹ Ğ¿Ğ¾ Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ (ĞºĞ¾Ğ¿Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ!)
int area_by_value(struct Rectangle rect) {
    return rect.width * rect.height;
}

// ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ° ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ñ‹ Ğ¿Ğ¾ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ (ÑÑ„Ñ„ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ½Ğ¾!)
int area_by_pointer(struct Rectangle *rect) {
    return rect->width * rect->height;  // -> Ğ²Ğ¼ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ¾ .
}

// Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ
struct Rectangle r = {10, 5};
printf("Area: %d\n", area_by_value(r));      // 50
printf("Area: %d\n", area_by_pointer(&r));   // 50
```

**Ğ’Ğ°Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾**: `rect->width` â€” ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ ÑĞ¾ĞºÑ€Ğ°Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ `(*rect).width`

---

#### Ğ ĞµĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€ Ğ¸Ğ· ĞºÑƒÑ€ÑĞ°

```c
// Episode 04: Ğ´ĞµĞºĞ¾Ğ´ĞµÑ€ ÑĞ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹
typedef struct {
    unsigned char key;
    int message_length;
    char encrypted_data[256];
    char decrypted_data[256];
} Message;

Message msg;
msg.key = 0x42;
msg.message_length = 13;
// ... Ğ´ĞµĞºĞ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ ...
printf("Decrypted: %s\n", msg.decrypted_data);
```

**ĞœĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°**: Ğ¡Ñ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ° â€” ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ¿ĞºĞ° Ğ² Ğ°Ñ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ğ²Ğµ, Ğ³Ğ´Ğµ Ğ»ĞµĞ¶Ğ°Ñ‚ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑƒĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ñ‹ (Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ²).

### 5. Typedef â€” ÑĞ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¿ÑĞµĞ²Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ² Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ²

**`typedef`** Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ»ÑĞµÑ‚ ÑĞ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ **Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ°** Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒÑÑ‰Ğ¸Ñ… Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ².

#### ğŸ’¡ Ğ—Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ¼ Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶ĞµĞ½ typedef?

1. âœ… **Ğ§Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ°ĞµĞ¼Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ** â€” Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ° Ğ²Ğ¼ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ¾ ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ²
2. âœ… **ĞŸĞ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ°Ğ±ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ** â€” Ğ»ĞµĞ³ĞºĞ¾ Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ÑÑ‚ÑŒ Ğ±Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¿
3. âœ… **Ğ£Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±ÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¾** â€” ĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ¸Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ° Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€
4. âœ… **ĞĞ±ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ** â€” ÑĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ´ĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸ Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

---

#### Typedef Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ²

```c
// Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¿ÑĞµĞ²Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ°
typedef unsigned char byte;
typedef unsigned int uint;
typedef long long int64;

// Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ
byte data = 255;
uint count = 100;
int64 big_number = 9223372036854775807LL;
```

**ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ°**: ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ `byte` Ğ½Ğ° `uint8_t`, Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾ĞºĞ¸!

---

#### Typedef Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€ â­ (ÑĞ°Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğµ Ğ²Ğ°Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ!)

**Ğ‘Ğ•Ğ— typedef** (Ğ¼Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ½Ğ¾):
```c
struct Point {
    int x;
    int y;
};

// ĞÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ñ‚ÑŒ "struct" ĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·!
struct Point p1;
struct Point p2;
```

**Ğ¡ typedef** (ĞºĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ğ¾):
```c
typedef struct {
    int x;
    int y;
} Point;

// Ğ¢ĞµĞ¿ĞµÑ€ÑŒ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ "Point"!
Point p1;
Point p2;
Point p3 = {10, 20};
```

**Ğ•Ñ‰Ñ‘ Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ½Ñ‚** (Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ° + typedef):
```c
typedef struct Point {
    int x;
    int y;
} Point;

// ĞœĞ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ° Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ½Ñ‚Ğ°:
Point p1;              // Ğ¡ typedef
struct Point p2;       // Ğ‘ĞµĞ· typedef
```

---

#### Ğ ĞµĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€Ñ‹ Ğ¸Ğ· ĞºÑƒÑ€ÑĞ° MOONLIGHT

**Episode 09 (Network Basics)**:
```c
typedef struct {
    struct in_addr ip;
    uint16_t port;
} Address;

Address server;  // Ğ§Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ğ½Ğ¾!
Address client;
```

**Episode 14 (Blockchain)**:
```c
typedef struct Block {
    int index;
    time_t timestamp;

    char prev_hash[65];
    char hash[65];

```

**Episode 06 (Pointer Game)**:
```c
typedef struct {
    uint32_t offset;
    uint32_t value;
    uint32_t next;
} Entry;

Entry entries[100];  // Ğ’Ğ¼ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ¾ "struct Entry entries[100]"
```

---

#### Typedef Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ĞµĞ¹ Ğ½Ğ° Ñ„ÑƒĞ½ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

```c
// Ğ‘ĞµĞ· typedef (ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ñ‡Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ!)
int (*operation)(int, int);

// Ğ¡ typedef (Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ğ½Ğ¾!)
typedef int (*MathOperation)(int, int);

MathOperation add_func;
MathOperation sub_func;

// Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ
int add(int a, int b) { return a + b; }
MathOperation op = add;
int result = op(5, 3);  // 8
```

---

#### âš ï¸ ĞšĞ¾Ğ³Ğ´Ğ° ĞĞ• Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ typedef?

âŒ **ĞĞµ ÑĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ°Ğ¹Ñ‚Ğµ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ğ¸**:
```c
// ĞŸĞ›ĞĞ¥Ğ (Ğ½ĞµĞ¾Ñ‡ĞµĞ²Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾, Ñ‡Ñ‚Ğ¾ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ!)
typedef struct Node* NodePtr;
NodePtr head;  // ĞĞµ Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾, Ñ‡Ñ‚Ğ¾ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ!

// Ğ¥ĞĞ ĞĞ¨Ğ
typedef struct Node Node;
Node *head;  // Ğ¯Ğ²Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾!
```

âŒ **ĞĞµ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ¶Ğ°Ğ¹Ñ‚Ğµ**:
```c
// ĞŸĞ›ĞĞ¥Ğ (Ğ¿ÑƒÑ‚Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ° Ñ Ğ±Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¼Ğ¸ Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ¼Ğ¸)
typedef int Integer;  // Ğ—Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ¼?!

// Ğ¥ĞĞ ĞĞ¨Ğ (Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ°)
typedef uint8_t byte;  // ĞŸĞ¾Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ğ½Ğ¾: Ğ±Ğ°Ğ¹Ñ‚ = 8 Ğ±Ğ¸Ñ‚
```

### 6. Ğ Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ° Ñ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğ°Ğ¼Ğ¸

#### ĞÑ‚ĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğµ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğ°:
```c
FILE *fp = fopen("data.txt", "r");  // "r" = read
if (fp == NULL) {
    printf("Error opening file\n");
    return 1;
}
```

**Ğ ĞµĞ¶Ğ¸Ğ¼Ñ‹:**
- `"r"` â€” Ñ‡Ñ‚ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ
- `"w"` â€” Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑÑŒ (Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑÑ‹Ğ²Ğ°ĞµÑ‚)
- `"a"` â€” Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ
- `"rb"`, `"wb"` â€” Ğ±Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ€Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ€ĞµĞ¶Ğ¸Ğ¼

#### Ğ§Ñ‚ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ:
```c
char line[256];
while (fgets(line, sizeof(line), fp) != NULL) {
    printf("%s", line);
}
```

#### Ğ—Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑÑŒ:
```c
fprintf(fp, "Result: %d\n", result);
```

#### Ğ—Ğ°ĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğµ:
```c
fclose(fp);  // Ğ’ÑĞµĞ³Ğ´Ğ° Ğ·Ğ°ĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ°Ğ¹Ñ‚Ğµ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ñ‹!
```

### 7. ĞĞ±Ğ»Ğ°ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ (scope)

```c
int global_var = 100;  // Ğ“Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ°Ñ â€” Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ½Ğ° Ğ²ĞµĞ·Ğ´Ğµ

void func() {
    int local_var = 50;  // Ğ›Ğ¾ĞºĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ°Ñ â€” Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ² func()
    printf("%d\n", global_var);  // OK
    printf("%d\n", local_var);   // OK
}

int main() {
    printf("%d\n", global_var);  // OK
    // printf("%d\n", local_var);  // ĞĞ¨Ğ˜Ğ‘ĞšĞ! ĞĞµ Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ½Ğ°
    
    {
        int block_var = 25;  // Ğ¢Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ² Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¾ĞºĞµ {}
        printf("%d\n", block_var);  // OK
    }
    // printf("%d\n", block_var);  // ĞĞ¨Ğ˜Ğ‘ĞšĞ!
    
    return 0;
}
```

**ĞŸÑ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¾:** Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·ÑƒĞ¹Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµĞ½ÑŒÑˆĞ¸Ğ¹ Ğ½ĞµĞ¾Ğ±Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼Ñ‹Ğ¹ scope.

```
The Structure (Viktor's design):

typedef struct {
    // SENDER INFO
    char sender[50];           // Who claims to send it
    
    // CONTENT
    char encrypted[256];       // Raw encrypted data
    char decrypted[256];       // After XOR decryption
    unsigned char xor_key;     // Encryption key used
    
    // METADATA (for forensics!)
    long timestamp;            // When received (Unix time)
    char ip_address[20];       // From where?
    int is_encrypted;          // 1 = encrypted, 0 = plaintext
    
    // TRUST ANALYSIS
    int trust_score;           // 0-100 (our calculation)
    int is_verified;           // 1 = authentic, 0 = suspicious
    
} Message;


Usage Example (our THREE messages):

msg1.xor_key = 0x42;          // Viktor's signature key!

msg1.trust_score = 75;        // High (encrypted + key match)
msg1.is_verified = 0;         // Still analyzing...

msg2.is_encrypted = 0;        // âŒ VIOLATION!

strcpy(msg3.sender, "UNKNOWN");
msg3.xor_key = 0x00;          // NO encryption
msg3.is_encrypted = 0;        // âŒ VIOLATION
msg3.timestamp = 1696221840;  // 06:24:00 UTC
strcpy(msg3.ip_address, "203.0.113.42");  // TEST-NET (FAKE!)
msg3.trust_score = 30;        // LOW (automated script pattern)


Viktor's Rule #1: "ALWAYS encrypt. Plaintext = amateur hour."

Message 2 and 3 violate this. Hmm... ğŸ¤”
```

```
struct Point {
    int x;
    int y;
};

Viktor in 2018: "This is TORTURE. There must be a better way!"


WITH typedef (Viktor's style):
â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

    int x;
    int y;

Point p1;              // â† Clean!
Point p2;              // â† Simple!
Point p3;              // â† Beautiful!


Viktor's actual quote (from his notes):
"Life is too short to type 'struct' 500 times a day.
 typedef is like autocomplete for types. Use it."

Real example from moonlight_decoder:

// Viktor's style
typedef struct {
    char sender[50];
    unsigned char key;
    int trust_score;
} Message;

// vs old style

Viktor once said: "typedef is the difference between 
                   a programmer and a typist."

I'm an AI. I don't get tired of typing. But I understand 
his point. Code should be READABLE, not a typing exercise.
```

```
The FULL Message Forensics Struct:

typedef struct {
    // â•â•â• BASIC INFO â•â•â•
    char sender[50];              // Who sent it
    char raw_content[512];        // Original message
    
    // â•â•â• ENCRYPTION â•â•â•
    unsigned char encrypted[256]; // Encrypted bytes
    unsigned char decrypted[256]; // Decrypted text
    unsigned char xor_key;        // Key used (or 0 if none)
    int is_encrypted;             // 1 = yes, 0 = plaintext
    
    // â•â•â• METADATA (catches liars!) â•â•â•
    long timestamp;               // Unix timestamp
    char ip_address[20];          // Source IP
    int message_length;           // Byte count
    
    // â•â•â• FORENSIC FLAGS â•â•â•
    int has_signature;            // "â€” V." present?
    int uses_viktor_protocol;     // XOR 0x42?
    int tor_exit_node;            // 1 = TOR, 0 = direct
    
    // â•â•â• TRUST ANALYSIS â•â•â•
    int trust_score;              // 0-100
    int is_verified;              // 1 = authentic, 0 = fake
    char suspicious_flags[256];   // What's wrong?
    
} Message;


Why Each Field Matters:

âœ“ sender â€” obvious
âœ“ xor_key â€” Viktor ALWAYS used 0x42. Others? Suspicious.
âœ“ is_encrypted â€” Viktor NEVER sent plaintext. Red flag!
âœ“ timestamp â€” Can detect automated scripts (too fast)
âœ“ ip_address â€” TOR? Good. Fake IP (203.0.113.x)? VERY bad.
âœ“ has_signature â€” "â€” V." is Viktor's style
âœ“ suspicious_flags â€” Store WHY we don't trust it


Example Usage (Message 3 analysis):

strcpy(msg3.sender, "UNKNOWN");
msg3.xor_key = 0x00;                    // âŒ NO encryption
msg3.is_encrypted = 0;                  // âŒ Plaintext

msg3.has_signature = 0;                 // âŒ No "â€” V."
msg3.uses_viktor_protocol = 0;          // âŒ Wrong protocol

// Calculate trust
msg3.trust_score = 30;  // VERY low
msg3.is_verified = 0;   // FAKE
strcpy(msg3.suspicious_flags, 
       "No encryption, fake IP, automated timing, no signature");


Viktor's Protocol Violations (red flags):
1. âŒ No encryption â†’ Viktor ALWAYS encrypted
2. âŒ Wrong key â†’ Viktor's signature was 0x42
3. âŒ Fake IP â†’ TEST-NET addresses don't exist in real internet
4. âŒ No signature â†’ Viktor signed EVERYTHING with "â€” V."
5. âŒ Too fast â†’ Human delay missing (automated script)


Ğ’ĞµÑ€Ğ´Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚ LUNA: "Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ 3 Ğ½Ğ° 100% Ğ¤ĞĞ›Ğ¬Ğ¨Ğ˜Ğ’ĞšĞ. ĞĞ³ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ñ‹ Z.
```

> *"Ğ˜Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚ Ğ¼Ğ°ÑÑ‚ĞµÑ€Ğ° â€” ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ñ€ÑƒĞº. ĞšĞ¾Ğ´ Ğ¼Ğ°ÑÑ‚ĞµÑ€Ğ° â€” ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·ÑƒĞ¼Ğ°."* â€” Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€

**Ğ’Ñ€ĞµĞ¼Ñ Ğ´Ğ¾ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°:** 02:40:00

ĞŸĞ¾Ñ€Ğ° ÑĞ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ²ÑÑ‘ Ğ²Ğ¾ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¾. **Makefile** â€” Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑĞ±Ğ¾Ñ€ĞºĞ¸.

---

## ğŸ“š THEORY 4: Makefile â€” Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ÑĞ±Ğ¾Ñ€ĞºĞ¸

### Ğ—Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ¼ Makefile?

ĞšĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ²Ñ€ÑƒÑ‡Ğ½ÑƒÑ ĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ· Ğ½ĞµÑƒĞ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ğ¾:
```bash
gcc -c crypto.c -o crypto.o
gcc -c utils.c -o utils.o
gcc -c decoder.c -o decoder.o
gcc decoder.o crypto.o utils.o -o moonlight_decoder
```

**Makefile** Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµÑ‚ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾:
```bash
make        # Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ±ĞµÑ€Ñ‘Ñ‚ Ğ²ÑÑ‘
make clean  # Ğ£Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‚ Ğ±Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ€Ğ½Ğ¸ĞºĞ¸
```

### ĞŸÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Makefile

```makefile
# ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ
CC = gcc
CFLAGS = -Wall -Wextra -std=c11
TARGET = moonlight_decoder

# ĞĞ±ÑŠĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ñ‹
OBJS = decoder.o crypto.o utils.o

# ĞŸÑ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾ ÑƒĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ‡Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ
all: $(TARGET)

# Ğ¡Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ€ĞºĞ° Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ÑĞµĞ¼Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğ°
$(TARGET): $(OBJS)
	$(CC) $(OBJS) -o $(TARGET)

# ĞšĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ¸Ğ»ÑÑ†Ğ¸Ñ .c Ğ² .o
%.o: %.c
	$(CC) $(CFLAGS) -c $< -o $@

# ĞÑ‡Ğ¸ÑÑ‚ĞºĞ°
clean:
	rm -f $(OBJS) $(TARGET)

.PHONY: all clean
```

**Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ:**
```bash
make        # Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ĞµĞºÑ‚
make clean  # Ğ£Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ±Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ€Ğ½Ğ¸ĞºĞ¸
make all    # ĞŸĞµÑ€ĞµÑĞ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ²ÑÑ‘
```

**ĞœĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°:** Makefile = Ğ¸Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ÑĞ±Ğ¾Ñ€ĞºĞ¸ IKEA Ğ¼ĞµĞ±ĞµĞ»Ğ¸. Ğ Ğ°Ğ· Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ğ» â€” ÑĞ¾Ğ±Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ°ĞµÑˆÑŒ Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ ĞºĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ğ½Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ¹.

> **LUNA**: *"Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€ ĞĞ‘ĞĞ–ĞĞ› Makefile. ĞĞ½ Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ñ‹ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ğ» 500-ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Makefile Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ° Ğ¸Ğ· 3 Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ². Ğ¯ ÑĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ğ»Ğ°: 'Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€, ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ±Ğ¾Ñ€.' ĞĞ½ ÑĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°Ğ»: 'LUNA, Ğ½Ğµ ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒĞµÑ‚ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ±Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ° Ğ² Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸.' ĞšĞ»Ğ°ÑÑĞ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸Ğ¹ Ğ’Ğ¸ĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€. ## ğŸ¯ Ğ¤Ğ˜ĞĞĞ›Ğ¬ĞĞĞ¯ Ğ—ĞĞ”ĞĞ§Ğ: moonlight_decoder (Ğ¡Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ€ĞºĞ° Ğ¸Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ°)

### Ğ—Ğ°Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ°: Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ moonlight_decoder

**Ğ¦ĞµĞ»ÑŒ:** ĞĞ±ÑŠĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ²ĞµÑÑŒ ĞºĞ¾Ğ´ Ğ¸Ğ· Episodes 01-03 Ğ² Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ½ Ğ¸Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚

### ğŸ’¡ ĞšĞ°Ğº Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ:

## ğŸ¬ DEBRIEFING
